hidden_albanian_border_highlighter={

	troop_deployment_in_border = {
		icon=alarm
		allowed={ tag=GRE }
        on_map_mode=map_only
        state_target = yes
        highlight_states={ highlight_state_targets={ state=FROM.id } highlight_color_while_active=1 highlight_color_before_active=1 }

        targets = { 185 973 }
        visible={
            divisions_in_border_state={ size>0 state=FROM.id border_state=805 }
            NOT={ has_active_mission=GRE_border_violations_epirus has_active_mission=GRE_border_violations_dytmak }
            NOT={ has_country_flag=disabled_troop_deployment_warning }
        }

        complete_effect={
            custom_effect_tooltip="Hide warning for 180 days"
            set_country_flag={ flag=disabled_troop_deployment_warning days=180 value=1 }
        }
	}
}

GRE_1936_election_category = {
	GRE_the_election_of_1936 = {                                                                        # Election crisis
		icon = eng_support_imperialist_coup
		allowed = { tag=GRE }
        on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
        highlight_states = { highlight_state_targets={ state=47 } highlight_color_while_active=1 }

		available={ hidden_trigger={ always=no }}
		activation={ check_variable={ GRE_election_1936<2 }}
        days_mission_timeout=var:GRE_1936_timeout_var?26
		days_remove=1
		is_good=yes

		timeout_effect = {
            if={
                limit={ check_variable={ GRE_election_1936=0 }}
            
                add_to_variable={ GRE_election_1936=1 }
                country_event={ id=hellenic_news.1 days=0 }
                remove_country_leader_trait=premier_in_crisis
                hidden_effect={ complete_national_focus=GRE_election_1936 }
                set_variable={ GRE_1936_timeout_var=35 }
            }
            else={
                hidden_effect = {
                    add_to_variable={ GRE_election_1936=1 }
                    country_event={ id=hellenic_news.2 days=7 }
                    complete_national_focus=GRE_georges_dictat
                    set_country_flag=GRE_faction_gui_flag
                    country_event={ id=hellenic_news.3 days=39 }
                    clear_variable=GRE_1936_timeout_var
                }
            }
		}
	}
}

    GRE_choosing_a_lignite_partner = {
        icon=oil
        allowed={ tag=GRE }
        highlight_states={ highlight_states_trigger={ state=FROM.capital }}
        targets={ ENG USA SOV GER }

		target_root_trigger={ 
			has_completed_focus=GRE_lignite_liquefaction
            has_completed_focus=GRE_open_up_the_country
		}

        available={
            has_completed_focus=GRE_expand_lignite_liq
            has_tech=synth_oil_experiments
			set_temp_variable={ dY=50 }
			has_paid_at_least_dY_debt=yes
            FROM={ has_opinion={ target=GRE value>60 }}
			set_temp_variable={ findX=FRA.id }
			set_temp_variable={ ftmpZ=60 }
			custom_trigger_tooltip={
				tooltip=favor_status_with_findX_at_least_ftmpZ_shrt_tt
				check_variable={ var=FRA.favor@GRE value=ftmpZ compare=greater_than_or_equals }
			}
        }

        visible={
            NOT={ has_variable=GRE_lignite_partner }
            NOT={ has_country_flag=toggle_adio }
        }

        cost=75
        fire_only_once=yes
        days_remove=14

        complete_effect={ set_variable={ GRE_lignite_partner=FROM.id }}
        
        remove_effect={
            if={
                limit={ FROM={ belongs_in_the_allied_sphere=yes }}
                set_temp_variable={ tmpT=0 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpQ=8 }
                tmpT_axal_by_tmpQ=yes
            }
            else_if={
                limit={ FROM={ belongs_in_the_axis_sphere=yes }}
                set_temp_variable={ tmpT=1 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpQ=8 }
                tmpT_axal_by_tmpQ=yes
            }
            FROM={
                custom_effect_tooltip=axal_nl_tt
                set_temp_variable={ favTT=2 }
                set_temp_variable={ findX=FROM }
                set_temp_variable={ findY=6 }
                fluctuate_favor_with_findX_by_findY=yes
                random_core_state={
                    add_extra_state_shared_building_slots=2
                    add_building_construction={
                        type=synthetic_refinery
                        level=2
                        instant_build=yes
                    }
                }
            }
            random_country={
                limit={ tag=GRE }
                if={
                    limit={ NOT={ has_tech=synth_oil_experiments }}

                    effect_tooltip={
                        random_owned_controlled_state={
                            prioritize={ 186 }
                            add_extra_state_shared_building_slots=2
                            add_building_construction={
                                type=synthetic_refinery
                                level=2
                                instant_build=yes
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                random_owned_controlled_state={
                    prioritize={ 186 }
                    limit={
                        free_building_slots={
                            building=synthetic_refinery
                            size > 0
                            include_locked=yes
                        }
                    }
                    add_extra_state_shared_building_slots=2
                    add_building_construction={
                        type=synthetic_refinery
                        level=2
                        instant_build=yes
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

GRE_economic_alleviation_category = {

	## Missions base: 365 (*10 = 3650)
	## Stability subtracts up to 100 days from base. Linearly. Gets us to 265.
    ## Each Metaxas' projects subtracts 5 from base apart from reducing current. If 30 total, then 150 days off. Gets us to 115.
    ## Each MEtaxas' Propaganda subtracts 10 from base apart from reducing current. If 10 total, then 100 days off. Gets us to 15.

    invigorating_hellenic_spirit = {
		icon=begging
        highlight_states = { highlight_state_targets={ state=47 }}

		allowed = { tag=GRE }
		activation = { has_completed_focus=GRE_utilize_our_strengths check_variable={ GRE.invigorating_level<1 }}
        available = { hidden_trigger={ always=no }}

		days_mission_timeout=365
		fire_only_once=no
		is_good = yes

		timeout_effect = {
            set_temp_variable={ decPROC=1 }
            improve_agrarian_dyn=yes 
        }
    }

		days_remove = 120

            if={ limit={ TUR={ exists=yes }} TUR={ capital_scope={ add_building_construction={ type=industrial_complex level=2 instant_build=yes }}}}
            if={ limit={ YUG={ exists=yes }} YUG={ capital_scope={ add_building_construction={ type=industrial_complex level=2 instant_build=yes }}}}
            if={ limit={ ROM={ exists=yes }} ROM={ capital_scope={ add_building_construction={ type=industrial_complex level=2 instant_build=yes }}}}
            if={ limit={ ALB={ has_country_flag=bed_gave_max exists=yes }} ALB={ capital_scope={ add_building_construction={ type=industrial_complex level=1 instant_build=yes }}}}
            if={ limit={ BUL={ has_country_flag=bed_gave_max exists=yes }} BUL={ capital_scope={ add_building_construction={ type=industrial_complex level=1 instant_build=yes }}}}
            if={ limit={ HUN={ has_country_flag=bed_gave_max exists=yes }} HUN={ capital_scope={ add_building_construction={ type=industrial_complex level=1 instant_build=yes }}}}

            hidden_effect={ every_country={ limit={ has_country_flag=bed_gave_max } clr_country_flag=bed_gave_max }}
        }
    }

	GRE_cut_our_ties = {
		icon = part_cut_ties

		allowed = { tag=GRE }
		available = { has_completed_focus=GRE_greek_autarky }
		ai_will_do = { factor=1 }
        
        visible = {
            OR = { has_idea=GRE_tied_to_foreign_investments has_idea=GRE_tied_to_foreign_investments_1 }
        }

        cost = var:GRE.cut_our_ties_cost
		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = 14

		complete_effect = {
            ###[ PP-Cost Increase ]###
            if={ limit={ check_variable={ has_idea=GRE_tied_to_foreign_investments }} add_to_variable={ GRE.cut_our_ties_cost=125 tooltip=increase_decision_base_cost_by }}
            else={ clear_variable=GRE.cut_our_ties_cost }
            ###[ Dynamic Impacts ]###
            set_temp_variable={ tot_infl=20 }
            # 1. World Tension (less = reduces influence lost)
            multiply_temp_variable={ x?100=global.threat } # max lost: 20 (has to be x100)
            set_temp_variable={ tmpTHR=0 }
            calculate_linearly_y_ax_b=yes
            multiply_temp_variable={ y=20 }
            add_to_temp_variable={ tot_infl=y }
            # 2. World Tension Caused (less = less influence lost)
            set_temp_variable={ x=GRE.has_added_tension_amount }    # max lost: 40                  
            calculate_linearly_y_ax_b=yes
            multiply_temp_variable={ y=40 }
            add_to_temp_variable={ tot_infl=y }
            # 3. Times Repeated (2nd time done is harsher)
            if={ limit={check_variable={ GRE.cut_our_ties_cost=150 }} add_to_temp_variable={ tot_infl=10 }}         #max lost: 10
            # 4. Debt Paid (more = less influence lost)
            set_temp_variable={ x=GRE.GRE_debt_to_the_ifc_paid_var_cat }        #max gained: 20
            calculate_linearly_y_ax_b=yes
            multiply_temp_variable={ y=20 }
            subtract_from_temp_variable={ tot_infl=y }
            #
            custom_effect_tooltip=cut_ties_influence_lost_tt
            log="Cutting Our Ties outcome:"
            hidden_effect={
                every_country = {
                    set_temp_variable = { findY=tot_infl }
                    multiply_temp_variable = { findY=-1 }
                    # 1. Influence with nation (more = reduces influence lost)
                    set_temp_variable={ x=THIS.favor@GRE }
                    calculate_linearly_y_ax_b=yes
                    multiply_temp_variable={ y=20 }
                    add_to_temp_variable={ findY=y }
                    #
                    clamp_temp_variable={ var=findY max=0 }
                    if={ limit={ original_tag=ITA } set_temp_variable={ ita_findY=findY }}
                    add_to_variable = { favor@GRE=findY }
                    log="  [?THIS.GetName] Lost [?findY] favor with [?y] saved."
                }
            }
            # 5. Escalation Event (ITA ONLY)
            ######[REPORT EVENTS]######
            add_to_temp_array = { tmpRECEIVERS=ITA.id }
            set_temp_variable = { tmpREAC1=52 }
            set_temp_variable = { b2=1 }
            multiply_temp_variable={ tmpMAG?-0.2=ita_findY }
            potentially_send_report_events_for_action_tmpREAC1_with_args_tmpARRVAL_tmpMAG_to_targets_tmpRECEIVERS = yes
            custom_effect_tooltip = report_event_diplomatic_reaction_due_to_x_tt
		}
        remove_effect={
            ###[ Improve Spirit ]###
            add_named_threat={ threat=3.0 name="Abruptly severed ties with the Investors" }
			improve_tied_economy_spirit = yes
        }
	}

            check_variable={ GRE.resource_choices_tungsten=0 }
            NOT={ has_decision=unearth_the_hidden_resources_tungsten }
        }

		fire_only_once=no
		days_remove=120
        
        modifier={ civilian_factory_use=6 }
        
        complete_effect={ subtract_from_variable={ GRE.resource_choices=1 }}
        remove_effect={ add_to_variable={ GRE.resource_choices_tungsten=1 }}
    }

		icon = commando_piazza
        on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
        highlight_states = { highlight_state_targets = { state = var:violations_varflag }}
		allowed = { tag=GRE }
		fire_only_once = no
        days_mission_timeout=30

        available = {
            set_temp_variable={ x=ITA.army_intel@GRE }
            clamp_temp_variable={ var=x min=0 max=100 }
            divide_temp_variable={ x=100 }
            set_temp_variable={ y=x }
            set_temp_variable={ x=150 }
            divide_temp_variable={ x=y }
            #############################################
            custom_trigger_tooltip={ tooltip=battalions_violation_tt has_exceeded_fielded_battalion_limit_based_on_italian_intel=no }
        }
		activation = {
            check_variable={ GRE.num_battalions>max_bats_allowed }
            NOT={ has_country_flag=bat_viol_intermission }
            has_war=no
            date<1942.1.1
            NOT={ has_global_flag=GRE_grecoitalian_ended }
            mussolini_historical_tensions_with_greece=yes
            has_country_leader={ ruling_only=yes character=GRE_ioannis_metaxas }

        cancel_if_not_visible = no
		is_good = no

            GRE = { add_political_power=-50 }
            ITA = { add_political_power=50 add_stability=0.01 add_war_support=0.01 }
        }
        
		timeout_effect = {
            if = {
                limit={ annexation_of_albania_has_occurred_one_way_or_another=yes }
                
                set_temp_variable={ tmpESC=25 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpACC=25 }
                apply_italian_aggression_effects_through_tmpESC_tmpACC_without_acceleration=yes
            }
            else = {
                add_political_power=40
                add_war_support=0.04
                set_country_flag={ flag=bat_viol_intermission days=14 value=1 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpESC=5.00 }
                set_temp_variable={ tmpACC=5.00 }
                apply_italian_aggression_effects_through_tmpESC_tmpACC=yes
                every_country = {
                    limit = { is_in_array={ array=global.favor_mechanic value=THIS.id }}

                    set_temp_variable={ findX=THIS.id }
                    set_temp_variable={ findY=-3 }
                    set_temp_variable={ favTT=2 }
                    fluctuate_favor_with_findX_by_findY=yes
                }
                custom_effect_tooltip="                                         "
            }
		}
	}

            GRE_budget_reduce_effects_by_tmpX_tokens=yes

    send_generals_to_get_used_with_land= {
		icon = salute

                }

        }

            set_temp_variable = { tmpMAG=0.80 }

                limit={ check_variable={ var=GRE_army_reform_cnt value=15 compare=less_than } has_idea=GRE_army_status_0 }
				swap_ideas={ remove_idea=GRE_army_status_0 add_idea=GRE_army_status_1 }
                set_variable={ GRE_ges=1 }
            }
            else_if={
                limit={ check_variable={ var = GRE_army_reform_cnt value = 15 compare = greater_than_or_equals } has_idea=GRE_army_status_0 }
				swap_ideas={ remove_idea=GRE_army_status_0 add_idea=GRE_army_status_2 }
                set_variable={ GRE_ges=2 }
            }
            else_if={ 
                limit={ has_idea=GRE_army_status_1 }
				swap_ideas={ remove_idea=GRE_army_status_1 add_idea=GRE_army_status_2 }
                set_variable = { GRE_ges = 2 }
            }
        }

                    set_temp_variable = { findX=THIS.id }
                    set_temp_variable_to_random = { var=findY min=1 max=2 }
                    fluctuate_favor_with_findX_by_findY=yes
                }
                every_country = {
                    limit = {
                        NOT = { tag=JAP tag=CHI tag=PRC }
                        is_major=yes
                        if = { limit={ FROM={ original_tag=CHI }} has_government=fascism }
                        else_if = { limit={ FROM={ original_tag=JAP }} NOT={ has_government=fascism }}
                        else = { has_government=fascism }
                    }
                    set_temp_variable = { findX=THIS.id }
                    set_temp_variable_to_random = { var=findY min=-4 max=-2 }
                    set_temp_variable={ favTT=2 }
                    fluctuate_favor_with_findX_by_findY=yes
                }
            }
            else = {
                custom_effect_tooltip=sija_tension_problems_warning_tt
            }
            custom_effect_tooltip="                                      "
        }
            
		remove_effect = {
            if={ limit={ FROM={ tag=JAP }} add_to_variable={ helped_the_japanese_magnitude=1 tooltip=increase_japanese_aid_tt }}
            else_if={ limit={ FROM={ tag=CHI }} add_to_variable={ helped_the_chinese_nationalists_magnitude=1 tooltip=increase_chinanat_aid_tt }}
            else_if={ limit={ FROM={ tag=PRC }} add_to_variable={ helped_the_chinese_communists_magnitude=1 tooltip=increase_chinacom_aid_tt }}
            else_if={ limit={ FROM={ is_in_faction_with=JAP }} add_to_variable={ helped_the_japanese_magnitude=0.5 tooltip=increase_japanese_aid_tt }}
            else_if={ limit={ FROM={ is_in_faction_with=CHI } FROM={ is_in_faction_with=PRC }} add_to_variable={ helped_the_chinese_nationalists_magnitude=0.25 tooltip=increase_chinanat_aid_tt } add_to_variable={ helped_the_chinese_communists_magnitude=0.25 tooltip=increase_chinacom_aid_tt }}
            else_if={ limit={ FROM={ is_in_faction_with=CHI } NOT={ FROM={ is_in_faction_with=PRC }}} add_to_variable={ helped_the_chinese_nationalists_magnitude=0.25 tooltip=increase_chinanat_aid_tt }}
            else_if={ limit={ NOT={ FROM={ is_in_faction_with=CHI }} FROM={ is_in_faction_with=PRC }} add_to_variable={ helped_the_chinese_communists_magnitude=0.25 tooltip=increase_chinacom_aid_tt }}
            ep_calculate_alignment=yes
            #########
            add_to_variable={ GRE.gold_reserves=0.5 tooltip=increase_gold_reserves_tt }
            add_to_variable={ irr=60 tooltip=increase_pyrkal_funds }
            clear_variable=irr
            hidden_effect={ mio:GRE_pyrkal_organization={ add_mio_funds=60 }}
            if={
                limit={ any_character={ is_character=GRE_prodromos_bodosakis check_variable={ trait_level<7 }}}

                add_to_variable={ GRE.bodosakis_experience=15 tooltip=bodosakis_experience_tt }
                calculate_bodosakis_experience_for_upgrade=yes
            }
            recalculate_gold_reserve_bonuses=yes
		}
    }

    ep_speak_in_favor_FROM = {
		icon = deals
        on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
        highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = FROM.capital } }
		allowed = { original_tag = GRE }
        targets = { JAP CHI PRC }
		cost = 0
        days_remove = 60

		fire_only_once = yes

		visible = {
			if={ limit={ FROM={ tag=CHI }} has_completed_focus=GRE_extend_arms_sales_to_the_chinese }
			if={ limit={ FROM={ tag=JAP }} has_completed_focus=GRE_arm_the_japanese }
			if={ limit={ FROM={ tag=PRC }} has_completed_focus=GRE_arm_the_communists }
		}
        
		available = {
            NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
            set_temp_variable = { tmpQ = 49 }
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip = ep_from_leading_alignment_by_tmpQ_tt
                check_variable = { GRE.ep_perc@FROM > tmpQ }
            }
        }
        
        complete_effect = {}
		remove_effect = {}
    }
}

#################[     Asfaleia     ]#################
#################[                  ]#################
######################################################
####[Breakdown]####
# Sub Tree A: Purge military from officers (Organize the Forces, Purge Communists, Purge Republicans, General Purge)
# Sub Tree B: Main Asfaleia Upgrade (Organize the Forces, Reinforce Gendarmerie, Fortify Asfaleia)
# Sub Tree B+: Domestic Persecutions (Arrest Communists, Arrest Democrats, Arrest Fascists)
# Sub Tree C: War on Domestic Ideologies
#          CA: War on Communism (Organize the Forces, First Arrest Wave, Zachariadis, Escalate Arrests, Ordeal of Castor Oil, Cooperate With Gestapo, Temporary Management, War on Communism) 
#          CB: War on Opposition (Organize the Forces, First Arrest Wave, Persecute Opposition, Deal with the Republican Threat, Deportation of embassy workers, Saving Eutaxias,) 
# Sub Tree D: War on Foreign Elements
#          DA: Persecution of Axis-aligned (Arrest of Alexandros Giannaros, )
# Sub Tree E: War on Minorities (Organize the Forces, War on Minorities, Chams, Slavs, Pomaks, Smooth Assimilation)
# Sub Tree F: Alternative/Grand Coallition (after reinforce, spy network, bonuses to intelligence etc.)
####[Political Power Cost]#####
# Before: 1350
# After: 1000 (full, without calculating benefits from purge).
# Sub Tree A: None, gives PP.
# Sub Tree B: 225 + 75 (common)
# Sub Tree C: 300 + 75 (common)
# Sub Tree D: 200 + 75 (common)
# Sub Tree E: 300
####[Time Cost]####

		icon = oppression

		visible = {

            custom_effect_tooltip = prop_dyn_up_tt

            add_to_variable={ GRE_var_drift_neutral=0.01 tooltip=prop_drift_neut_tt }

                limit={ has_country_flag=GRE_faction_gui_flag }
                
                set_temp_dem_insignificant_positive = yes
                set_temp_com_slightly_detrimental = yes
                set_temp_fas_slightly_beneficial = yes
                set_temp_mon_slightly_beneficial = yes
            }
            ###[AXAL MECHANIC]###
            set_temp_variable = { tmpQ=1 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = axal_increase_by_tmpQ
            add_to_variable = { GRE.axal = tmpQ }
            axal_gui_call = yes
            ######[REPORT EVENTS]######
            set_temp_variable = { tmpREAC1=60 }
            set_temp_variable = { tmpREAC2=61 }
            set_temp_variable = { CM=1 }
            set_temp_variable = { CD=0 }
            set_temp_variable = { CC=2 }
            set_temp_variable = { CF=1 }
            set_temp_variable = { b1=40 }
            set_temp_variable = { b2=60 }
            set_temp_variable = { tmpIMP=0.1 }
            potentially_send_report_events_for_actions_tmpREAC1_tmpREAC2_with_args_tmpARRVAL_tmpMAG_and_code = yes
            custom_effect_tooltip = report_event_warning_potential_repercussions_diplomatic_tt
            ###
            hidden_effect = { set_country_flag=red_literature_decided }
        }

        remove_effect = {
            add_to_variable={ amount_of_work_in_propaganda=1 tooltip=propaganda_work_increased_tt }
            ############[ BoP MECHANICS ]#############
            set_temp_variable={ tmpMOV=0.025 }
            fluctuate_bop_by_tmpMOV_tmpTT=yes
            ###[ FACTION MECHANICS ]###
            if={
                limit={ has_country_flag=GRE_faction_gui_flag }
                
                set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect_increase = 8 }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = fct_mon_effect_multiplier }
                add_to_temp_variable = { tmp_mon_effect = tmp_mon_effect_increase }
                set_variable = { fct_mon_effect_multiplier = tmp_mon_effect }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp_com_effect_decrease = 8 }
                set_temp_variable = { tmp_com_effect = fct_com_effect_multiplier }
                subtract_from_temp_variable = { tmp_com_effect = tmp_com_effect_decrease }
                set_variable = { fct_com_effect_multiplier = tmp_com_effect }
                #########  ############
                custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_title
                custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_up_mon
                custom_effect_tooltip = GRE_fct_effect_multiplier_change_shrt_down_com
            }
        }

		icon = democracy
        #priority = 70329
        priority = 5

		allowed = { tag=GRE }

            date > 1938.09.01
            has_country_flag = GRE_protected_eng_telecom
		}

            has_country_flag = GRE_protected_eng_telecom
		}

            add_to_variable = { ENG.favor@GRE = 10 }
            custom_effect_tooltip = declare_will_to_befriend_british_tt
            hidden_effect = {
                every_country = {
                    limit = {
                        is_in_array = {
                            array = global.favor_mechanic
                            value = THIS.id
                        }
                    }
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            is_in_faction_with = ENG
                        }
                        add_to_variable = { THIS.favor@GRE = 10 }
                    }
                    else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            OR = {
                                original_tag = GER
                                original_tag = ITA
                            }
                            NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
                        }
                        subtract_from_variable = { THIS.favor@GRE = 10 }    
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    escape_the_schachtplan = {
		icon=indep
		allowed={ tag=GRE }
        highlight_states={ highlight_states_trigger={ state=GRE.capital }}

		available={ has_country_flag=balkan_pact_reinforced }

		visible={
            NOT={ has_country_flag=toggle_ebl }
            has_completed_focus=GRE_the_balkan_pact

                has_idea=GRE_schachtplan_modified
                has_idea=GRE_schachtplan_stabilized
            }
		}

		fire_only_once=yes
        days_remove=7
        
        remove_effect = {
            custom_effect_tooltip=escape_the_schachtplan_tt
            hidden_effect={
                if={ limit={ has_idea=GRE_schachtplan_stabilized } swap_ideas={ remove_idea=GRE_schachtplan_stabilized add_idea=GRE_schachtplan_incorporated }}
                else={ swap_ideas={ remove_idea=GRE_schachtplan_modified add_idea=GRE_schachtplan_incorporated }}
            }            
            set_temp_variable = { findX = GER }
            set_temp_variable = { findY = -15 }
            fluctuate_favor_with_findX_by_findY=yes
            set_temp_variable = { tmpT = 0 }
            set_temp_variable = { tmpQ = 6 }
            tmpT_axal_by_tmpQ = yes
            ###[ BOP MECHANIC ]###
            set_temp_variable={ tmpMOV=0.10 }
            fluctuate_bop_by_tmpMOV_tmpTT=yes
            ###[ ITAGG ]###
            if={
                limit={ german_italian_collaboration_exists=yes }

                set_temp_variable={ tmpESC=7.5 }
                add_to_temp_variable={ tmpACC=15 }
            }
            else={ 
                set_temp_variable={ tmpESC=4 }
                add_to_temp_variable={ tmpACC=8 }
            }
            apply_italian_aggression_effects_through_tmpESC_tmpACC=yes
            custom_effect_tooltip=escalation_dynamic_affect_pact_of_steel
        }
    }

    bp_subsidized_factories = {
        icon = industry
        allowed = { tag = GRE }
        on_map_mode = map_only
        highlight_states = { highlight_states_trigger = { state = FROM.capital } }
        
        targets = {	TUR YUG ROM BUL ALB }

		target_trigger = {
            country_exists = FROM
			FROM = { has_country_flag = balkan_pact_reinforced }
            NOT = { has_global_flag = GRE_grecoitalian_start }
            NOT = { has_axis_occupation = yes }
		}

        available = {
            GRE = { num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 10 }
            FROM = {
                has_political_power > 50 
                custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                    tooltip = no_gsfc_tt
                    NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GRE_greek_subsidized_factories_cost } }
                }
            }
        }

        visible={
            NOT={ has_country_flag=toggle_ebl }
        }

        fire_only_once = no
        days_remove = 60

        modifier = { civilian_factory_use = 10 }

        complete_effect = {
            add_political_power = 200                           ### We get payed upfront, cause we ain't dummies
            ####################################                ### Phase 1, they pay base 50 upfront
            set_variable = { FROM.gre_gsfc = -0.75 }                ### Phase 2, they pay base 45 daily (45/60=0.75)
            set_variable = { FROM.gre_ifd  = 5 }                 ## They also contribute with 5 civs
            FROM = {
                add_political_power = -50
                add_dynamic_modifier = {
                    modifier = GRE_greek_subsidized_factories_cost
                    days = 270
                }
                custom_effect_tooltip = gsfc_tt
            }
        }

        remove_effect = {
            set_variable = { FROM.gre_gsfc = -0.5 }         ### They pay the rest 105 over 210 days.
            set_variable = { FROM.gre_ifd = 0 }              ## Their civ contribution is over
            FROM = {
                set_temp_variable = { findX = FROM.id }
                set_temp_variable = { findY = 10 }
                set_temp_variable = { favTT = 2 }
                fluctuate_favor_with_findX_by_findY=yes
                set_temp_variable={ tmpAW=4.00 } 
                add_to_variable = { balkan_pact_desirability=tmpAW } 
                refresh_balkan_pact_desirability_gui_THIS=yes
                custom_effect_tooltip = alliance_weight_increased_tmpAW_tt
                random_owned_controlled_state = {
                    add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
                    add_building_construction = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 instant_build = yes }
                    add_building_construction = { type = arms_factory level = 1 instant_build = yes }
                }
                clear_variable = gre_ifd
            }
            add_to_variable = { GRE.civs_given@FROM = 1 }
            add_to_variable = { GRE.mils_given@FROM = 1 }
        }
    }

            }

        }

	GRE_comm_upr = {
		icon = faction_gre_communist
        on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
        highlight_states = {
 			highlight_state_targets = { state = 185 } 
 			#highlight_color_before_active = 3
			highlight_color_while_active = 1
		}
		allowed = { tag = GRE }

		available = {
            set_temp_variable={ tmpZ=40 }
            custom_trigger_tooltip={
                tooltip=comm_uppr_dealt_tt
                OR={ com_is_at_least_tmpZ=yes has_country_flag=communist_uprising_utterly_crushed }
            }
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 95
        fire_only_once = yes
		activation = { has_country_flag = GRE_comm_upr_1 }
        visible = { has_country_flag = GRE_comm_upr_1 }
		cancel_if_not_visible = no
		is_good = no

		complete_effect = {
            clr_country_flag = GRE_comm_upr_1
            add_stability = 0.02
            add_to_variable = { fct_com = 2.5 }
            faction_gui_call = yes
		}

		timeout_effect = {
            set_temp_variable = { x = party_popularity@communism }
            ###[Take the highest between Representation and Overall Military Grip]###
            set_temp_variable = { y = GRE.com_asgn_w }
            multiply_temp_variable = { y = 0.04 }
            set_temp_variable = { tmpF = 2 }
            calculate_mg_percentage = yes
            if = { limit = { check_variable = { y < mg } } set_temp_variable = { y = mg } }
            ###[Multiply and Clamp]###
            multiply_temp_variable = { x = y }
            clamp_temp_variable = {
                var = x
                min = 0.02
                max = 0.85
            }
            ###[Start Civil War]###
            start_civil_war = {
                ruling_party = ROOT
                ideology = communism
                size = x
                capital = 47
                states = { 185 972 973 }
                keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { has_trait = trait_GRE_stauch_communist_persona }
                keep_political_leader = yes
            }
            set_country_flag = com_civilwar_started
		}
	}

GRE_balance_of_power_category={
    GRE_bop_promises_of_accomplishments={
        icon=metaxas

        fire_only_once=yes
        days_remove=365
        available={ 
            set_temp_variable = { tmpPR=4 }
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip=more_than_tmpPR_projects
                check_variable = { var=amount_of_projects value=tmpPR compare=greater_than_or_equals }
            }
        }
        
        complete_effect={
            set_variable={ bop_promises_of_accomplishments_start_num=amount_of_projects }
            set_temp_variable={ tmpMOV=0.005 }
            fluctuate_bop_by_tmpMOV_tmpTT=yes
        }

        #modifier={
        #    fct_dem_effect_multiplier_modifier_token = -0.01
        #    fct_com_effect_multiplier_modifier_token = -0.01
        #    fct_fas_effect_multiplier_modifier_token = -0.01
        #    fct_mon_effect_multiplier_modifier_token = 0.03
        #}

        remove_effect = {
            if={ limit={ NOT={ has_variable=bop_promises_of_accomplishments_start_num }} custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_bop_promises_of_accomplishments_succ_tt }
            else={
                set_temp_variable={ x=bop_promises_of_accomplishments_start_num }
                add_to_temp_variable={ x=5 }
                custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_bop_promises_of_accomplishments_run_tt 
            }
            if={
                limit={
                    if={
                        limit={ has_variable=bop_promises_of_accomplishments_start_num }
                    
                        set_temp_variable={ x=bop_promises_of_accomplishments_start_num }
                        add_to_temp_variable={ x=5 }
                        check_variable={ var=amount_of_projects value=x compare=greater_than_or_equals }
                    }
                }

                add_stability=0.02
                ###[ BOP MECHANIC ]###
                set_temp_variable={ tmpMOV=0.095 }
                fluctuate_bop_by_tmpMOV_tmpTT=yes
                ###################################
                if = {
                    limit = { OR={ has_active_mission=GRE_repub_upr has_active_mission=GRE_comm_upr has_active_mission=workers_entering_factories has_active_mission=invigorating_hellenic_spirit }}
                    
                    custom_effect_tooltip = mis_impacts_header
                }
                if = {
                    limit = { has_active_mission = GRE_repub_upr }

                    set_temp_variable={ tmpMISS=1 }
                    set_temp_variable={ tmpSIGN=0 }
                    set_temp_variable={ tmpARD=90 }
                    set_temp_variable={ tmpDIS=90 }
                    custom_effect_tooltip = mis_impact
                    hidden_effect={ add_days_mission_timeout={ mission=GRE_repub_upr days=tmpARD }}
                }
                if = {
                    limit = { has_active_mission = GRE_comm_upr }

                    set_temp_variable={ tmpMISS=0 }
                    set_temp_variable={ tmpSIGN=0 }
                    set_temp_variable={ tmpARD=90 }
                    set_temp_variable={ tmpDIS=90 }
                    custom_effect_tooltip = mis_impact
                    hidden_effect={ add_days_mission_timeout={ mission=GRE_comm_upr days=tmpARD }}
                }
                if = {
                    limit = { has_active_mission=workers_entering_factories }

                    set_temp_variable={ tmpMISS=2 }
                    set_temp_variable={ tmpSIGN=0 }
                    set_temp_variable={ tmpARD=-30 }
                    set_temp_variable={ tmpDIS=30 }
                    custom_effect_tooltip = mis_impact
                    hidden_effect={ add_days_mission_timeout={ mission=workers_entering_factories days=tmpARD }}
                }
                if = {
                    limit = { has_active_mission=invigorating_hellenic_spirit }

                    set_temp_variable={ tmpMISS=3 }
                    set_temp_variable={ tmpSIGN=0 }
                    set_temp_variable={ tmpARD=-30 }
                    set_temp_variable={ tmpDIS=30 }
                    custom_effect_tooltip = mis_impact
                    hidden_effect={ add_days_mission_timeout={ mission=invigorating_hellenic_spirit days=tmpARD }}
                }
                ###[ FACTION MECHANICS ]###
                if={
                    limit={ has_country_flag=GRE_faction_gui_flag }
                    
                    set_temp_dem_beneficial = yes
                    set_temp_com_beneficial = yes
                    set_temp_fas_beneficial = yes
                    set_temp_mon_beneficial = yes
                }
  
                set_temp_variable={ extra=amount_of_projects }
                subtract_from_temp_variable={ extra=bop_promises_of_accomplishments_start_num }
                subtract_from_temp_variable={ extra=5 }
                if={
                    limit={ check_variable={ extra>0 }}

                    multiply_temp_variable={ extra_stab?0.010=extra }
                    multiply_temp_variable={ extra_bop?0.015=extra }
                    hidden_effect={ 
                        add_stability = extra_stab
                        set_temp_variable={ tmpMOV=extra_bop }
                        fluctuate_bop_by_tmpMOV_tmpTT=yes
                    }
                    custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_bop_promises_of_accomplishments_extra_tt
                }
            }
            if={ limit={ NOT={ has_variable=bop_promises_of_accomplishments_start_num }} custom_effect_tooltip=GRE_bop_promises_of_accomplishments_fail_tt }
            if={
                limit={
                    if={
                        limit={ has_variable=bop_promises_of_accomplishments_start_num }
                    
                        set_temp_variable={ x=bop_promises_of_accomplishments_start_num }
                        add_to_temp_variable={ x=5 }
                        check_variable={ var=amount_of_projects value=x compare=less_than }
                    }
                }

                add_stability=-0.05
                ###[ BOP MECHANIC ]###
                set_temp_variable={ tmpMOV=-0.1 }
                fluctuate_bop_by_tmpMOV_tmpTT=yes
                ###[ FACTION MECHANICS ]###
                if={
                    limit={ has_country_flag=GRE_faction_gui_flag }
                    
                    set_temp_dem_almost_catastrophic = yes
                    set_temp_com_almost_catastrophic = yes
                    set_temp_fas_almost_catastrophic = yes
                    set_temp_mon_almost_catastrophic = yes
                }
            }
        }
    }

    
    GRE_bop_emergency_regime_stabilization={
        icon=metaxas

        fire_only_once=yes
        days_remove=90
        available={ is_power_balance_in_range={ id=GRE_power_balance range<stabilized_0 }}
        
        complete_effect={
            ###[ FACTION MECHANICS ]###
            if={
                limit={ has_country_flag=GRE_faction_gui_flag }
                
                set_temp_dem_adverse = yes
                set_temp_com_adverse = yes
                set_temp_fas_adverse = yes
                set_temp_mon_favourable = yes
            }
        }

        modifier={
            fct_dem_effect_multiplier_modifier_token = -0.10
            fct_com_effect_multiplier_modifier_token = -0.10
            fct_fas_effect_multiplier_modifier_token = -0.10
            fct_mon_effect_multiplier_modifier_token = 0.30
            political_power_gain = -0.15
            power_balance_weekly = 0.002
        }
    }

    GRE_bop_add_debug = {
        icon=metaxas
        
        visible={ is_debug=yes }
        fire_only_once=no

        complete_effect={
            set_temp_variable={ tmpMOV=0.15 }
            fluctuate_bop_by_tmpMOV_tmpTT=yes
        }
    }
}

            event_target:hellenic_state = { set_country_flag = requested_german_intervention }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { GER.favor@GRE > 79 }
                }
                event_target:hellenic_state = { add_political_power = 100 }
            }
            else_if = {
                limit = {
                    check_variable = { GER.favor@GRE > 49 }
                }
                event_target:hellenic_state = { add_political_power = 75 }
            }
            else = {
                event_target:hellenic_state = { add_political_power = 50 }
            }
        }
    }

		on_map_mode = map_only
		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = 0

		visible = {
            FROM = { 
                FROM = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = black_market_ubshakeable } }
            }
            NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_black_market_icons }
            OR = {
                has_country_flag = black_market_option_invest
                has_country_flag = black_market_option_crackdown 
            }
		}
		remove_effect = {
            if = { 
                limit = { has_country_flag = black_market_option_crackdown } 
                FROM = { HS_BM_reduce_level = yes }
                if = { limit = { FROM = { state = 47 } } add_political_power = -150 }
                else_if = { limit = { FROM = { OR = { state = 974 state = 731 state = 186 state = 971} } } add_political_power = -125 }
                else = { add_political_power = -100 }
            }
		}
	}

        icon = decision_generic_decision
    
        allowed = { tag=GRE }
        
        fire_only_once = no
        days_remove = 0
        days_re_enable = 0
        priority = 10
        
        visible = { has_axis_occupation=yes }
        
        complete_effect = {
            hidden_effect = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_unyielding_greeks_icons }
                    }
                    set_country_flag = hide_unyielding_greeks_icons
                }
                else = {
                    clr_country_flag = hide_unyielding_greeks_icons 
                }
            }
        }
    }
